 party supremeo mulaayam singh yadav or party ke uttar pradesh ke pramukh shivpal yadav ne yah nirnay sunaaya or phir pehali baar mulaayam singh yadav or soobe ke mukhiya akhilesh yadav ke bich jari manmutav logon ke saamne aayaa
 Before this, Shivpal Yadav had also merged the party of Communist Party of India (mukhtar Ansari) with SP, which Akhilesh Yadav did not like
 sapa apane puraane andaaj main muslim vot bank ke chalate purvi uttar pradesh main apni pakad ko majboot karne ke liye yah kadam uthaa rahi thi, to mukhyamantri akhilesh yadav yah nahin chaahate the ki phir party par bahubali ke dam par chalane kaa aarope lage
 Akhilesh Yadav and Shivpal Yadav got upset over this issue
 akhilesh ke dabaav main ansaari kii party se vilay samaapt kiya gaya or phir bhale hi baad main mulaayam singh yadav ne shivpal yadav kaa saath diya or vilay phir ho gaya
 Akhilesh Yadav was seen standing completely with his uncle Professor Ram Gopal Yadav and father and party chief Mulayam Singh Yadav with his brother Shivpal Yadav
 mulaayam singh ne saaf kaha ki party ke liye shivpal yadav ne kaam kiya or ramgopal ne party ke liye kuch nahin kiya
 At the same time, Ram Gopal Yadav said that he has done a lot in strengthening the party and raising the party from the casteism
 itnaa hi nahin ramgopal yadav ne daawa bhi kiya ki party kaa samvidhan bhi unhone taiyaar kiya he
 His expulsion was later canceled after Ram Gopal Yadav apologized (as per Mulayam Singh Yadav's claim) on a public forum
 kuch samay pehle kii is ghatana ke baad shuukravaar kii shaam phir pita-putr main vivaad aayaa

 xxrep 104 - bete akhilesh yadav ko party se nikaalane ke paksh main nahin the pita mulaayam singh yadav
 
 
 xxrep 50 - xxrep 50 - xxrep 4 - isse naaraaz party pramukh mulaayam singh yadav ne professor ramgopal yadav ko party se chah saal ke liye phir nishkasit kar diya or saath hi unhone shivpal yadav kii salaah par mukhyamantri akhilesh yadav ko bhi party se chah saal ke liye nishkasit kar diya
 With the announcement of Mulayam Singh Yadav on the evening of 30 December, it was decided that the time has come to test the power in the party and it is to be decided who is more popular in the party, who is the future of the party and whom the public There is more acceptability in which party mlas trust is maintained
 30 disambar kii shaam se 31 disambar ke dopaher tak shakti pradarshan kaa daur chalaa or yah saaf ho gaya ki party main kiski chalegi
 Who is the future of the party party, netaa or kaaryakarta kiske saath janaa chaahate hai
 The assembly of mlas started at Akhilesh's house since morning
 khabar ai ki akhilesh yadav ke ghar par 200 se zyada vidhayakon ne aamad kii or sarkaar ke sabhi mantri bhi vahaan pahunche
 Not only this, there was an overnight gathering of Akhilesh supporters outside Mulayam Singh Yadav's house
 ve sabhi lagaataar akhilesh ke samarthan main naare lagaate rahe
 According to sources, Akhilesh Yadav went to the house of his father and party chief Mulayam Singh Yadav after taking the details of the mlas who came in his support and clarified the present situation in front of him
 donon ke bich kya baatcheet hui yah to saaf nahin he
 But within minutes of this meeting, it was pointed out by Mulayam Singh Yadav that the party had canceled the expulsion of Akhilesh Yadav and Professor Ram Gopal Yadav from the party
 party main akhilesh ke nishkasana ke radd hone saath hi yah saaf ho gaya ki party main akhilesh yadav kaa bolbalaa rahegaa
 The party will follow the path shown by them
 vaise raajnneetik jaankaron kaa maananaa he ki mulaayam singh yadav bete akhilesh yadav ko nishkasit nahin karnaa chaahate the, lekin shivpal yadav ke dabaav main liya gaya kadam party main varchasv kii ladaai ke rup main badal jayega, yah kisi ko andaja nahin tha
 Akhilesh Yadav did not take his step back and forced the party chief to withdraw his expulsion for not more than 24 hours
 akhilesh yadav ne apni sharton par apni vaapasi kii ghoshnaa karwaai or iske sabake baad professor ramgopal yadav ne phir saaf kar diya he ki ghoshit kiya gaya apaat sammelan (mahadhiveshan) apane samay par 1 janvari ko baqayada yojit hoga
 It is clear from this that Akhilesh Yadav has won in the battle of supremacy in the party
 vahiin, yah bhi saaf he ki ab mulaayam singh yadav raajnneetik vanvaas jane se batch gaye

 tippaniyan Do you know about the fact that a dinosaur was also named after Rabindranath Tagore? Indian forest officer Parveen Kaswan has shared this unique fact on Twitter with all the information
 ham or aap jitani kalpana kar sakate hai, bharat kaa itihaas usase kahin zyada vividhta se bharaa he
 Let us tell you that dinosaur fossils were first discovered in India in the year 1828
 ise baad main kolkata or landan ke sangrahalayon main bheja gaya tha, lekin kya aap jaanate hai ki inamen se ek dianasor kaa naam rabindranath tagore ke naam par bhi rakhaa gaya tha
 An Indian Forest Service (indian Forest Service) officer Parveen Kaswan has posted this information along with the facts on Twitter
 apane post main unhone puure vivaran kaa bhi ullekh kiya
 Do you know # rabindranathtagore has a dinosaur named after him
 Barapasaurus # tagoreiwas a 18 metre long & 7 tonned # dinosaurwhich walked through # Indiaonce
 It was the first complete mounted dinosaur skeleton discovered in 1960s in Adilabad district of # India
 — Parveen Kaswan, IFS (@parveenkaswan)october 22, 2019unhone apane twit main likhaa ki "kya aap jaanate hai rabindranath tagore ke naam par ek dianasor he? barapasoras # tagorei ek 18 meter lanbaa or 7 ton kaa # audionsaur tha jo ek baar # India se gujara tha
 It was the first complete dinosaur skeleton discovered in Adilabad in Adilabad district in 1960

 Barapasaurus # tagoreiwas a 18 meter long & 7 tonned # dinosaurwhich walked through # Indiaonce
 It was the first complete mounted dinosaur skeleton discovered in 1960s in Adilabad district of # India
 - Parveen Kaswan, IFS (@parveenkaswan) October 22, 2019 The Barapasaurus or big-leopard Lizard is taken from a bar or a large one while Pa refers to the foot
 suras ek greek shabd he jo chhipakali main tabdeel hota he
 In this way, Tagorei in the Barapasaurus Tagorai is in honor of the distinguished poet-writer

 maamle kii sunwaayee kar rahe nyaayamurti aftab alam ne bina nyaayalay ko soochna die niyukti karne par gujarat sarkaar se sawaal jawaab kiya
 Justice said that canceling the appointment of Judge Vyas does not mean questioning his allegiance
 sarvocch nyaayalay ne iske baad yachikakarta biji vargeez evam geetkaar javed akhtar or gujarat sarkaar se praadhikaran ke pramukh ke liye naam kaa suzav dene ko kaha
 The comments is par javed akhtar ke adhivaktaa prashanth bhushan ne sarvocch nyaayalay ke avkaash praapt nyaayamurti bi
 Proposed the name of Sudarshan Reddy
 jabaki gujarat sarkaar ke adhivaktaa ranjit kumaar ne kuch samay kii maang kii
 The next hearing of the case has been postponed till Monday

 Appa Rao, a farmer from Guntur in Andhra Pradesh, sold his kidney when he had no choice
 30 saal ke is kisaan Sold his kidney about a year ago
 use tab dalal dwaara kaha gaya tha ki kidney ke liye saadhe chaar lakh rupee die jaaenge
 The broker showed all the papers to Appa and told him that the whole process was being done under the law
 un kagajaton main tamaam sarkari adhikariyon or doctoron ke dastakhat the
 In all these papers, it was said that Appa Rao donated his kidneys because of his love for the recipient
 is prakriya ke puure hone ke baad appa raav ko maatr ek tihaai rakam hi di gai
 Appa Rao, stating the reason for the decision to 'sell' his kidney, said that in 2009 his crop was completely destroyed due to rain
 phir chota kaarobaar karne ke liye appa ne bazaar main nijee vyavsaayee se oonche byaaj par paisa liya tha
 Monthly fees were very high due to interest
 iske baad jaise hi kidney bechney kaa prastaav appa nakaar nahin paae
 When Appa discussed this in her house, her wife and mother refused to do anything like this but i said that now there is no other option but to commit suicide
 appa ne kaha, dalal ne dhokhaa diya or kareeb do lakh se zyada rupaya nahin diya
 But now i can not say anything to anyone
 ab meri sehat kharaab ho chuki he
 Can not work
 mujhe apana gaanv chhodana padaa he or naam chhupaakar rahanaa pad rahaa he
 Let us tell that in Guntur, Andhra Pradesh, all farmers cultivate chilli and cotton
 sookhaa, tufaan or gaiyr-mausami barish ne unki fasal ko chaupat kar diya he
 The locals do not mind the story of Appa Rao much
 palanadu ilaake ke bhi tamaam kisaanon kii bhi lagbhag yahi kahani he
 The situation has now become that some have started doing brokerage work themselves
 in maamalon kaa kagajaat bataate hai ki kidney nikaalane kii surgery hyderabad ke bade aspataalon main kii gai he or puri kanoonee prakriya kaa paalan karte hue
 Many kidney sellers are not even ready to tell their name
 unhen lagata he ki aisa karne se ve khud kanoonee pachade main funs jaaenge
 The comments varisht police adhikari kaa kahana he ki in maamalon main karrwai karke bhi koi phayda nahin hoga kyonki court main kagajaat par sab nirbhar karata he
 So far, not a single case has been filed in these cases
 rajya ke maanavadhikaar ayog ne ab sarkaar ko likhaa he ki maamle kii puri jaanch kar vaastavik sthiti par report den
 The Commission has asked how the extradition of human organs in this way is going on illegally

 party ke kai netaa isse khaase naaraaz hai
 Already Kejriwal and angry leaders from the party have publicly attacked, now the leaders sitting in senior positions in the party have also shown public displeasure
 party kii ore sansad main bheje gaye sanjay singh ne is prakaran main arvind kejariwal se duuri bana lee he

 lekin unhone phir saaf kaha ki main apni baat par kaayam hum ki majithia drugs dealer he or use jail janaa chahie

 padhein :bhagwant maan ne diya AAP party pad se istipha, arvind kejariwal kii bikram majithia se maafee se the naaraaz Arvind Kejriwal's Aam Aadmi Party, whose leaders have more than 20 defamation cases, has decided to settle those cases
 kejariwal apane upar chal rahe sabhi manahani ke maamalon ko khatm karne ke liye sabhi sambadhit netaaon se baat karenge

 ' In order to promote fixed line phone connections in the country, the Telecom Regulatory Authority of India (TRAI) has removed the fee paid by the landline service provider to other service providers for communicating their consumer's calls
 isse landline kol kii daron main kami aane kii sambhaavna he
 Now, there will be no interconnection fee for calling landline to landline or landline to mobile, which is 20 paise
 iske alaava doorsanchaar niamak ne mobile phone ke jariye kiye jane vaali colls par network interconection yuses charge (aiusi) ko kareeb 30 pratishat ghataakar 20 paise se 14 paise kar diya he
 a customer of a telecom company has to pay an interconnection fee when he calls on another network

 Let me tell you, this study has been completed by researchers from Carnegie Malone University and University of Kansas
 shodhakartaaon ne 5 stadiyon kaa ekasaath adhyan karte hue is rirpot ko taiyaar kiya he
 It has also been revealed in this report that sharing your relationships more on social media can also cause problems in your relationship
 study main kaha gaya ki soshal media par khud ke bare main yaa apni vyaktigat jaankaree adhik baar saajha karne se aapke partner ke man main ye dharna ban sakati he ki aapaki life main unka khaasaa mahattav nahin he
